def five_multiples(num_list):
  x = []
  for i in num_list:
    if i % 5 == 0:
      x.append(i)
  return x
def five_multiples(num_list):
    s = []
    for i in num_list:
        if i % 5 == 0:
            s.append(i)
    return s
def five_multiples(num_list):
    nas=[]
    for i in num_list:
        if not(i%5):
        	nas.append(i)
    return nas

def five_multiples(num_list):
    s=[]
    for i in num_list:
        if i%5==0: s.append(i)
    return s

def five_multiples(num_list):
    output = []
    for maybe in num_list:
        if not (maybe % 5):
            output.append(maybe)
    return output

def five_multiples(num_list):
    temp_list = []
    for i in range(len(num_list)):
        if(num_list[i] % 5 == 0):
            temp_list.append(num_list[i])
    return temp_list
def five_multiples(num_list):
    x = []
    for i in num_list:
        if i % 5 == 0:
            x.append(i)
    return x

def five_multiples(num_list):
    nasobky_peti = []
    for i in range(len(num_list)):
        if (num_list[i]) % 5 == 0:
            nasobky_peti.append(num_list[i])
    return nasobky_peti
def five_multiples(num_list):
    new_list = []
    for i in range(len(num_list)):
        if num_list[i]%5 == 0:
            new_list.append(num_list[i])
    return new_list

def five_multiples(num_list):
    five_folds=[]
    for x in num_list:
        if x%5==0:
            five_folds.append(x)

    return five_folds

def five_multiples(num_list):
    my=[]
    for char in num_list:
        
        if char%5==0:
            my.append(char)
    return my

    for numbers in num_list:
        if numbers % 5 == 0:
            output.append(numbers)
    return output

def five_multiples(num_list):
    nasobky = []
    for i in num_list:
        if i%5==0:
            nasobky.append(i)
    return nasobky

def five_multiples(num_list):
    new_list = []
    for number in num_list:
        if number % 5 == 0:
            new_list.append(number)
    return new_list
            
def five_multiples(num_list):
    five_multi = []
    for i in range(len(num_list)):
        if num_list[i] % 5 == 0:
            five_multi.append(num_list[i])
    return five_multi

def five_multiples(num_list):
    seznam = []

        if i%5==0:
            seznam.append(i)
    
    return seznam

    for x in num_list:
        if x%5==0:
            five_folds.append(x)

    return five_folds

def five_multiples(num_list):
    my=[]
    for char in num_list:
        
        if char%5==0:
            my.append(char)
    return my
            
def five_multiples(num_list):
    array = []
    for t in num_list:
        if t % 5 == 0:
            array.append(t)
    return array

def five_multiples(num_list):
    r = []
    for item in num_list:
        if item % 5 == 0:
            r.append(item)

    return r

def five_multiples(num_list):
    b = []
    a = 0
    for i in range(len(num_list)):
        if num_list[i]%5==0:
            b.append(num_list[i])
            
    return b

def five_multiples(num_list):
    x = []
    for i in range(len(num_list)):
        if num_list[i] % 5 == 0:
            x.append(num_list[i])
    return x

    for i in num_list:
        if i%5 == 0:
            new.append(i)
    return new

def five_multiples(num_list):
    new_list = []
    for item in num_list:
        if item % 5 ==0:
            new_list.append(item)
    return new_list

def five_multiples(num_list):
    return_list = []
    for i in num_list:
        if i % 5 == 0:
            return_list.append(i)
    return return_list

def five_multiples(num_list):
    output = []
    for numbers in num_list:
        if numbers % 5 == 0:
            output.append(numbers)
    return output

def five_multiples(num_list):
    five_multi = []
    for i in range(len(num_list)):
        if num_list[i] % 5 == 0:
            five_multi.append(num_list[i])
    return five_multi

    for i in range(0, len(num_list)):
        if num_list[i] % 5 == 0:
        	result.append(num_list[i])    
    return result

def five_multiples(num_list):
    five_mul = []
    for i in num_list:
        if i % 5 == 0:
            five_mul.append(i)

    return five_mul
def five_multiples(num_list):
    new_num_list = []
    for i in num_list:
        if i % 5 == 0:
            new_num_list.append(i)
    return new_num_list

    for i in num_list:
        if i % 5 == 0:
            s.append(i)
    return s
def five_multiples(num_list):
    nas=[]
    for i in num_list:
        if not(i%5):
        	nas.append(i)
    return nas

def five_multiples(num_list):
    s=[]
    for i in num_list:
        if i%5==0: s.append(i)
    return s

def five_multiples(num_list):
    output = []
    for maybe in num_list:
        if not (maybe % 5):
            output.append(maybe)
    return output

def five_multiples(num_list):
    temp_list = []
    for i in range(len(num_list)):
        if(num_list[i] % 5 == 0):
            temp_list.append(num_list[i])
    return temp_list
def five_multiples(num_list):
    x = []
    for i in num_list:
        if i % 5 == 0:
            x.append(i)
    return x

def five_multiples(num_list):
    nasobky_peti = []
    for i in range(len(num_list)):
        if (num_list[i]) % 5 == 0:
            nasobky_peti.append(num_list[i])
    return nasobky_peti
def five_multiples(num_list):
    new_list = []
    for i in range(len(num_list)):
        if num_list[i]%5 == 0:
            new_list.append(num_list[i])
    return new_list

def five_multiples(num_list):
    five_folds=[]
    for x in num_list:
        if x%5==0:
            five_folds.append(x)

    return five_folds

def five_multiples(num_list):
    my=[]
    for char in num_list:
        
        if char%5==0:
            my.append(char)
    return my

    array = []
    for t in num_list:

            array.append(t)
    return array

    for item in num_list:
        if item % 5 ==0:
            new_list.append(item)
    return new_list

def five_multiples(num_list):
    return_list = []
    for i in num_list:
        if i % 5 == 0:
            return_list.append(i)
    return return_list

def five_multiples(num_list):
    output = []
    for numbers in num_list:
        if numbers % 5 == 0:
            output.append(numbers)
    return output

def five_multiples(num_list):
    nasobky = []
    for i in num_list:
        if i%5==0:
            nasobky.append(i)
    return nasobky

def five_multiples(num_list):
    new_list = []
    for number in num_list:
        if number % 5 == 0:
            new_list.append(number)
    return new_list
            
def five_multiples(num_list):
    five_multi = []
    for i in range(len(num_list)):
        if num_list[i] % 5 == 0:
            five_multi.append(num_list[i])
    return five_multi

    for i in num_list:
        if i % 5 == 0:
            alist.append(i)
            
    return alist

def five_multiples(num_list):
    res = []
    for num in num_list:
        if num % 5 == 0:
            res.append(num)
    return res

def five_multiples(num_list):
    multiples = []
    for i in num_list:
        if i % 5 == 0:
            multiples.append(i)
    return multiples

def five_multiples(num_list):
    new = []
    for number in num_list:
        if number % 5 == 0:
            new.append(number)
    return new

def five_multiples(num_list):
    fives = []
    for x in num_list:
        if x % 5 == 0:
            fives.append(x)
    return fives

def five_multiples(num_list):
    multiples = []
    for i in range(len(num_list)):
        if num_list[i] % 5 ==0:
            multiples.append(num_list[i])
            
    return multiples

    for n in l:
        if n%5==0:
            nl.append(n)
    return nl

def five_multiples(num_list):
    l = []
    for x in num_list:
        if x % 5 == 0:
            l.append(x)
    return l

def five_multiples(num_list):
    new_num_list = []
    for number in num_list:
        if number % 5 == 0:
            new_num_list.append(number)
    return new_num_list

def five_multiples(num_list):
    new = []
    for p in num_list:
        if p % 5 == 0:
            new.append(p)
    return new

def five_multiples(num_list):
    div_by_five = []
    for i in num_list:
        if i % 5 == 0:
            div_by_five.append(i)
    return div_by_five

def five_multiples(num_list):
    newlist = []
    for i in num_list:
        if i % 5 == 0:
            newlist.append(i)
    return newlist

def five_multiples(num_list): # vypíše ze seznamu čísla dělitelná 5ti.
    alist = []
    for i in num_list:
        if i % 5 == 0:
            alist.append(i)
    return alist

            new.append(i)
    return new

def five_multiples(num_list):
    new = []
    for item in num_list:
        if item%5 == 0:
            new.append(item)
    return new

def five_multiples(num_list):
    result = []
    for i in range(0, len(num_list)):
        if num_list[i] % 5 == 0:
        	result.append(num_list[i])    
    return result

    for i in range(len(num_list)):
        if num_list[i]%5 == 0:
            div5.append(num_list[i])
    return div5

def five_multiples(num_list):
    five_list = []
    for n in num_list:
        if n % 5 == 0:
            five_list.append(n)
    return five_list
            

def five_multiples(num_list):
    new = []
    for i in num_list:
        if i%5 == 0:
            new.append(i)
    return new

def five_multiples(num_list):
    new_list = []
    for item in num_list:
        if item % 5 ==0:
            new_list.append(item)
    return new_list

    return output
